19       given your bereavement and your heart problems. I hope                   19
20       the heart problems resolve soon.                                         20
21   PROFESSOR ALEXANDER: That's very kind of you, my Lady.                       21
22   LADY HALLETT: And thank you too, Mr Mann, for being here                     22
23       too.                                                                     23
24                          (The witnesses withdrew)                              24
25   MR KEITH: Thank you, my Lady, that concludes today's                         25
